1.555h21.777a1.556 1.556 0 0 0 1.556-1.555V6.222a1.557 1.557 0 0 0-.093-.474ZM4.394 21.778h-1.08v-1.112l5.654-5.608 1.096 1.096-5.67 5.624Zm20.697 0h-1.089l-5.67-5.623 1.097-1.097 5.654 5.608.008 viewBox="11.01 11.02 23.98 23.96" fill="#0B3558" stroke="#0B3558"><path fill="none" stroke="currentStroke" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2.438" d="M20.833 24.083a5.416 fDQloc"><p font-size="s20" font-weight="bold" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 jAkAfA">Experience scheduling automation for yourself!</p><p font-size="s16" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 ejxNZ">Create a Calendly account in seconds.</p><div direction="column" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 jHdkod"><a data-testid="primary-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dCoJlx" href="/signup"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx">Sign up for free</span></a></div></div></div></div><div direction="column" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 jUioWV"><div width="100%" height="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 sc-d54a3bd1-0 gHLXBH iIduIB"><div data-testid="callout-section" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 jOxrUi"><div width="100%" height="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 iiSnrV"><div data-testid="callout-conversion-panel" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 iiTDiY"><div direction="column" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 jUioWV"><h4 data-testid="callout-conversion-panel-title" font-size="s28" font-weight="semiBold" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 jafAqy">What is lead management?</h4><div data-testid="callout-conversion-panel-body" width="100%" height="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 sc-7ddf7a40-0 ktJgKx jEMXq">Lead management is the process of collecting, organizing, tracking, and nurturing potential customers from lead generation to conversion. With lead management, sales teams can capture leads’ information, follow where they are in the sales cycle, and guide them through the process of becoming a customer.</div></div></div></div></div><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Your sales team does more than prospect, qualify leads, and conduct meetings. Admin tasks like assigning, organizing, and tracking leads take up valuable time that could be spent connecting with prospects and closing deals.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">If a long sales cycle is making it hard to hit your numbers, you’re not alone. The <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://databox.com/b2b-sales-cycle-length" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">median B2B sales cycle length is 2.1 months</span></span></a></span>! Luckily, effective lead management processes mean that repetitive tasks won’t slow down the buyer’s journey or disrupt deals.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">In this guide, we’ll cover everything you need to know about lead management, from the stages in the lead process to the software that makes up a lead management system. We’ll walk through six lead management best practices, then explore how Calendly can make lead management easier, faster, and more effective for your team.</p><h2 id="Why-do-you-need-lead-management?" class="sc-372af2a2-0 dqpylw">Why do you need lead management?</h2><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Lead management helps sales and marketing teams:</p><ul class="sc-9f52a7fd-1 buUria"><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Reach interested prospects faster (before the competition!)</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Focus on the most valuable leads</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Stop qualified prospects from slipping through the cracks</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Spend less time on time-consuming tasks like manual lead assignment</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Create personalized experiences that lead to <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/blog/sales-conversion-rate-strategy"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">higher sales conversion rates</span></span></a></span> and happier customers</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/blog/accelerate-sales-pipeline-scheduling-automation"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Speed up your entire sales pipeline</span></span></a></span> to close more deals, faster</p></li></ul><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Plus, you get tons of data about your customers, sales processes, lead sources, and marketing campaigns, so your team can make data-driven decisions going forward.</p><h2 id="Stages-of-the-lead-management-process" class="sc-372af2a2-0 dqpylw">Stages of the lead management process</h2><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">A typical lead management process follows these steps:</p><ol class="sc-9f52a7fd-2 kxVxVi"><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Lead generation:</b> Identify potential customers and get their attention. Lead gen often involves activities like paid ads, content marketing, and social media.</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Lead capture: </b>Gather contact information from interested leads. Lead capture usually involves a web form — the “contact us” form on your website, a piece of gated content, a webinar registration landing page, etc.</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Lead tracking:</b> After generating leads, it's important to keep track of their interactions with your website, content, and emails. This info helps you understand how interested a lead is in your product.</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Lead scoring:</b> Assign leads scores based on their behavior, demographics, and other factors. Lead scoring helps sales teams prioritize the leads that are most likely to convert.</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Lead qualification: </b>Determine how likely a lead is to become a customer based on their level of interest, how well the product fits their needs, and how ready they are to buy. Like lead scoring, lead qualification processes help sales teams focus on the most promising leads.&nbsp;</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Lead nurturing:</b> Guide qualified leads through the buying process with tailored content, personalized interactions, and targeted messaging.</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Lead distribution: </b>Once leads are qualified and scored, assign them to the right sales rep or team. This step is also often called <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/blog/lead-routing"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">lead routing</span></b></span></a></span>.</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Lead conversion:</b> Close the deal! Then, <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/blog/seamless-handoff-sales-to-customer-success"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">hand off the customer to your customer success team</span></span></a></span>.</p></li></ol><h2 id="Types-of-leads" class="sc-372af2a2-0 dqpylw">Types of leads</h2><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">As you learn more about lead management, you’ll hear different types of leads referred to by a variety of terms and acronyms. Here are some of the most common.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Inbound leads:</b> Inbound leads are prospective customers who have initiated contact with your business by filling out a website form, downloading a piece of gated content, or reaching out directly to your sales team. In other words, they’re leads who come to you.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Outbound leads: </b>Outbound leads are leads your sales team reaches out to first via cold phone calls or emails.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Information qualified leads (IQLs): </b>These leads are at the top of your sales funnel and haven’t yet shown much interest or engagement. For example, an IQL visits your website and views a few pages but doesn’t download gated content or sign up to learn more. IQLs are sometimes called <b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">cold leads</b>.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Product qualified leads (PQLs): </b>PQLs have already experienced your product in some way and have shown interest in buying or upgrading. If you offer a free trial, a PQL might be someone who uses your product every day during the trial period.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Marketing qualified leads (MQLs): </b>These leads have engaged with your marketing. An MQL could be someone who downloaded a whitepaper or e-book from your website, showing interest in a particular topic related to your product. MQLs are sometimes called <b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">warm leads</b>.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Sales qualified leads (SQLs): </b>These leads have shown more interest, are a better fit for your product, and are ready to buy soon. For example, a lead who requests a demo, engages with your sales emails, and requests a pricing quote is an SQL. SQLs are sometimes called <b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">hot leads</b>.</p><h2 id="What-is-a-lead-management-system?" class="sc-372af2a2-0 dqpylw">What is a lead management system?</h2><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">A lead management system is software that helps businesses keep track of prospects, from when they first show interest to when they become paying customers. Lead management tools help sales and marketing teams organize their leads, decide which ones are most likely to buy, and keep all the important info about each lead in one place.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Automation is a big part of what makes lead management systems so useful for sales and marketing teams. The best lead management software helps teams automate time-consuming tasks like qualifying, nurturing, and distributing leads.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Your lead management system might be one piece of software, like a CRM, or a whole tech stack of different tools, including:</p><ul class="sc-9f52a7fd-1 buUria"><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Customer relationship management (CRM) software (like <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://www.salesforce.com/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Salesforce</span></span></a></span> or <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://www.freshworks.com/crm/sales/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Freshsales</span></span></a></span>)</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Pipeline management tools (like <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://www.pipedrive.com/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Pipedrive</span></span></a></span> or <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://www.zoho.com/crm/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Zoho CRM</span></span></a></span>)</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/blog/marketing-automation"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Marketing automation software</span></span></a></span> (like <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://www.hubspot.com/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">HubSpot</span></span></a></span>, <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Marketo</span></span></a></span>, or <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" imAMjQ">Gong</span></span></a></span>)</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Workflow automation platforms (like <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://zapier.com/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Zapier</span></span></a></span>)</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Data enrichment tools (like <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://clearbit.com/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Clearbit</span></span></a></span> or <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://www.zoominfo.com/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">ZoomInfo</span></span></a></span>)</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/blog/lead-routing"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Lead routing</span></span></a></span> software (like <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/features/routing"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Calendly</span></span></a></span>)</p></li></ul><h3 id="Lead-management-software-vs.-CRM-software" class="sc-372af2a2-0 hihnyK">Lead management software vs. CRM software</h3><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Lead management software refers to tools that focus on the lead lifecycle, from generation to conversion. These tools are usually designed for sales and marketing teams.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Most CRMs address the entire customer journey, including retention, and are often used by customer success teams alongside sales and marketing. Many CRM systems, like Salesforce, have <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/blog/salesforce-lead-management"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">lead management features built in</span></span></a></span>.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">That said, there’s definitely some overlap between the two categories — don’t worry too much about trying to choose between them. Instead, focus on finding the lead management solution that fits your team’s processes, budget, and goals.</p><h2 id="Lead-management-examples" class="sc-372af2a2-0 dqpylw">Lead management examples</h2><h3 id="Calendly’s-lead-management-system" class="sc-372af2a2-0 hihnyK">Calendly’s lead management system</h3><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">What does a real-life lead management tech stack look like? Here are some of the lead management automation tools Calendly’s marketing and sales teams use — and why:</p><ul class="sc-9f52a7fd-1 buUria"><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://business.adobe.com/products/marketo/adobe-marketo.html" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Marketo</span></span></a></span>: For communicating with sales leads. We use it for lead scoring, lead nurture campaigns, educational content, and “talk to sales” CTAs.&nbsp;</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://www.salesforce.com/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Salesforce</span></span></a></span>: Salesforce is our source of truth when it comes to lead and customer info. It integrates with the rest of our tech stack (<span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/integration/salesforce"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">including Calendly</span></span></a></span>!), so everything stays up-to-date and consistent.</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://clearbit.com/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Clearbit</span></span></a></span>: We use Clearbit to help us understand more about our leads and customers, like their industry, company size, and location. It also hides form fields when we already have the customer info, shortening the forms for a better user experience.</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://salesloft.com/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Salesloft</span></span></a></span>: For sales email sequences from Calendly reps to individual prospects.</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://www.gong.io/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Gong</span></span></a></span>: For customer intelligence. Gong records sales calls, tracks sales activities, and gives us visibility into our pipeline.</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Calendly</span></span></a></span>: For scheduling and <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/blog/lead-routing"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">lead routing</span></span></a></span>. We use Calendly links as CTAs in our sales emails, so prospects can schedule with sales ASAP. <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/features/workflows"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Automation workflows</span></span></a></span> let us automatically send SMS and email reminders and follow-ups before and after events. We also use <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/features/routing"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Calendly Routing</span></span></a></span> to route qualified leads to the right booking page instantly.</p></li></ul><h3 id="How-Searchant-automated-their-lead-processes" class="sc-372af2a2-0 hihnyK">How Searchant automated their lead processes</h3><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://www.searchant.co/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Searchant</span></span></a></span> is a digital marketing agency helping businesses grow their organic traffic. The Searchant sales team had a manual lead intake process, which was incredibly time-consuming for reps and made it difficult to handle an increasing number of leads. Scaling the business seemed impossible.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Then, the Searchant team added Calendly and Zapier to their lead management process. Zapier creates automatic workflows — called Zaps — across different software.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Searchant created a Zap to automate the admin tasks that made lead intake so cumbersome. When a new lead books a meeting through Calendly, the Zap:</p><ul class="sc-9f52a7fd-1 buUria"><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Instantly sends a pre-sell email to the lead</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Adds the lead to Searchant’s CRM</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Sends a message to the Searchant sales team member scheduled to take the call</p></li></ul><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Now, every lead gets tracked while minimizing manual data entry. The results? Ten hours saved every month and a 25% decrease in no-shows.</p><div data-testid="callout-section" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 jOxrUi"><div width="100%" height="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 iiSnrV"><div direction="column" data-testid="callout-testimonial" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 hFlcTa"><h3 font-weight="semiBold" class="sc-372af2a2-0 eLJaNK">“<!-- -->Adding automation to your processes means a few small changes can lead to massive time savings each month. This saved time is yours to play with, and can be used to alleviate your workload and drive you towards growth.<!-- -->”</h3><div data-testid="callout-testimonial-person" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 kXCqii"><div width="100%" display="flex" class="sc-dd2631d-0 gicXsq"><div width="100%" height="64px" class="sc-dd2631d-0 sc-bf28344b-0 eiiQPC fOFzJS next-image-wrapper" src="https://images.ctfassets.net/k0lk9kiuza3o/3Mj28HrlM9ofPE738WofBn/a776099ef8e15d117108f043d56af7db/MarcusClarke.jpeg?q=85&amp;fm=webp" style="color: transparent; object-fit: cover;"></div></div><div width="100%" height="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 iOpdhU"><p font-size="s20" font-weight="semiBold" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 fkEhjj">Marcus Clarke</p><p class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 fHWosc">Founder<!-- --> <!-- -->at<!-- --> <!-- -->Searchant</p></div></div></div></div></div><div data-testid="callout-section" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 jOxrUi"><div width="100%" height="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 iiSnrV"><div data-testid="callout-switchback" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 iiTDiY"><div overflow="hidden" data-testid="callout-switchback-image" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 cqdiqK"><div width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 sc-bf28344b-0 kvHEiz bTbbHj next-image-wrapper" display="flex"><img alt="E-book: 4 ways to automate your lead management" loading="lazy" width="0" height="0" decoding="async" data-nimg="1" style="color:transparent;object-fit:contain" src="https://images.ctfassets.net/k0lk9kiuza3o/SvxqrhQRLYiiIvekXZiGe/72b4da28ec8361d12e176383d2dfe807/-Ebook-_Calendly_x_Zapier.png?q=85&amp;fm=webp"></div></div><div direction="column" width="100%" display="flex" class="sc-dd2631d-0 dhjnTZ"><div display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 bhbaoe"><h4 data-testid="callout-switchback-title" font-size="s28" font-weight="semiBold" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 jafAqy">E-book: 4 ways to automate your lead management</h4></div><div data-testid="callout-switchback-body" width="100%" height="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 sc-eaa94a81-0 eFMMXe bDJlSh">Fill pipeline, stop leads from slipping through the cracks, and save time on admin tasks with lead management automation.<div class="sc-dd2631d-0 sc-9f52a7fd-5 kXCqii beZgaB button-container" width="100%" display="flex"><a data-testid="primary-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dCoJlx" href="/resources/ebooks/automate-lead-management"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx">Get the e-book</span></a></div></div></div></div></div></div><h2 id="6-lead-management-best-practices" class="sc-372af2a2-0 dqpylw">6 lead management best practices</h2><h3 id="1.-Focus-on-the-right-prospects-with-lead-qualification" class="sc-372af2a2-0 hihnyK">1. Focus on the right prospects with lead qualification</h3><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Your team's time is valuable — what if you could guarantee they spend it on high-quality leads?</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">That's where <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/blog/lead-qualification"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">lead qualification</span></span></a></span> comes into play.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Not every inbound lead is the right fit for your product. If you sent every form fill directly to a sales rep, your team would spend a good chunk of their time talking to leads who may never convert.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Lead qualification determines how likely a sales prospect is to become a customer based on their level of interest, how well the product fits their needs, and how ready they are to make a purchase. With an effective lead qualification process, your team can focus on the most promising leads, <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/blog/accelerate-sales-pipeline-scheduling-automation"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">speeding up the sales cycle</span></span></a></span>.&nbsp;</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">To know whether a lead fits your ideal buyer persona, you first have to <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://www.gartner.com/en/articles/the-framework-for-ideal-customer-profile-development" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">define your ICP</span></span></a></span>. What makes someone a great fit for your product? What are some telltale signs they're ready to buy (and have the authority and budget to make it happen)?</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Your ICP should include job titles, company size, industry, location, demographics, pain points, and existing tech stack. Depending on your product, you may have multiple ICPs in different industries.</p><div data-testid="callout-section" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 jOxrUi"><div width="100%" height="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 iiSnrV"><div direction="column" data-testid="callout-testimonial" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 hFlcTa"><h3 font-weight="semiBold" class="sc-372af2a2-0 eLJaNK">“<!-- -->We use lead qualification to ensure the right leads are getting to our sales team, with the right message, at the right time.<!-- -->”</h3><div data-testid="callout-testimonial-person" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 kXCqii"><div width="100%" display="flex" class="sc-dd2631d-0 gicXsq"><div width="100%" height="64px" class="sc-dd2631d-0 sc-bf28344b-0 eiiQPC fOFzJS next-image-wrapper" display="flex"><img alt="Testimonial author" loading="lazy" width="800" height="800" decoding="async" data-nimg="1" src="https://images.ctfassets.net/k0lk9kiuza3o/1aEhqcvdtnS9Xo7HojKkVf/006325840ce585b760d16369a504546e/KorynDelPrince.jpeg?q=85&amp;fm=webp" style="color: transparent; object-fit: cover;"></div></div><div width="100%" height="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 iOpdhU"><p font-size="s20" font-weight="semiBold" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 fkEhjj">Koryn DelPrince</p><p class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 fHWosc">Manager, Lifecycle Marketing<!-- --> <!-- -->at<!-- --> <!-- -->Calendly</p></div></div></div></div></div><h3 id="2.-Set-up-lead-scoring" class="sc-372af2a2-0 hihnyK">2. Set up lead scoring</h3><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/lead-scoring-instructions" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Lead scoring</span></span></a></span> lets you quantify how engaged and qualified a lead is as they move through the buyer’s journey.&nbsp;</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">You can identify and track the most promising leads by assigning values to actions like website visits, content downloads, demo bookings, or email interactions. Lead management tools like Salesforce, Marketo, and ActiveCampaign simplify lead scoring setup and monitoring.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">At Calendly, we use lead scoring to determine which leads should be routed to the sales team, and when. Here’s one example:</p><ol class="sc-9f52a7fd-2 kxVxVi"><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">A new lead fills out a form on the landing page for a piece of gated content.</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">The lead enters Marketo, which we use for lead nurture and scoring.</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Depending on the lead’s industry, title, and other characteristics, we use segmentation to send nurture emails with content related to their interests and needs.</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">The lead scores points based on activities, like replying to a sales email or booking a meeting.</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">When the lead hits a score of 100, they’re routed to the sales team to book a meeting.</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Once they’re qualified by a sales rep, they become a sales-qualified opportunity and continue through the sales process.</p></li></ol><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Lead scoring ensures sales reps prioritize warm or hot leads who’ve demonstrated real purchase intent. Sales pro Armand Farrokh, Founder of <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://www.30mpc.com/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">30 Minutes to President’s Club</span></span></a></span> (30MPC), says sending lukewarm leads right to AEs is a common lead routing error: “The biggest mistake you can make is trying to get an enterprise AE to work [new] e-book leads, then complaining when your time to first touch is 27 days.”</p><div data-testid="callout-section" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 jOxrUi"><div width="100%" height="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 iiSnrV"><div direction="column" data-testid="callout-testimonial" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 hFlcTa"><h3 font-weight="semiBold" class="sc-372af2a2-0 eLJaNK">“<!-- -->Use the right channel based on the lead temperature. Cold leads? Let marketing warm them up. Warm leads? Let an SDR pull them into a meeting. Hot leads? Get them in the hands of an AE now.<!-- -->”</h3><div data-testid="callout-testimonial-person" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 kXCqii"><div width="100%" display="flex" class="sc-dd2631d-0 gicXsq"><div width="100%" height="64px" class="sc-dd2631d-0 sc-bf28344b-0 eiiQPC fOFzJS next-image-wrapper" display="flex"><img alt="Testimonial author" loading="lazy" width="800" height="800" decoding="async" data-nimg="1" src="https://images.ctfassets.net/k0lk9kiuza3o/2fXP6Kt32mkPCENKPsEe5P/ae05b9d1d86f42dc1b9b364a1108f758/ArmandFarrokh.jpeg?q=85&amp;fm=webp" style="color: transparent; object-fit: cover;"></div></div><div width="100%" height="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 iOpdhU"><p font-size="s20" font-weight="semiBold" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 fkEhjj">Armand Farrokh</p><p class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 fHWosc">Founder<!-- --> <!-- -->at<!-- --> <!-- -->30 Minutes to President's Club</p></div></div></div></div></div><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">(Looking for more sales insights from the 30MPC team? <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/resources/ebooks/sales-script-templates"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Check out these templates and scripts for every meeting in the sales journey</span></span></a></span>.)</p><h3 id="3.-Gather-the-right-data-via-your-marketing-forms" class="sc-372af2a2-0 hihnyK">3. Gather the right data via your marketing forms</h3><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Add the right fields to your marketing forms to collect important info about leads. You need more than a name and email address to put your new lead management strategy into action! Plus, you need to understand a lead’s company size, industry, and pain points for lead qualification.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Asking all those questions up front would make for a pretty cumbersome form, and long-form answers are time-consuming for your team to read and analyze. Luckily, when you know which job titles, industries, and company sizes tend to make a good lead, you can use dropdown menus to collect that valuable info without overwhelming prospects.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Depending on your tech stack, you may be able to use data enrichment tools like <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://clearbit.com/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Clearbit</span></span></a></span> and <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://www.zoominfo.com/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">ZoomInfo</span></span></a></span> to shorten your marketing forms while still collecting all the info you need to route leads. Clearbit provides verified B2B company and contact info, then dynamically shortens your forms accordingly. Does Clearbit already know how large the company is? If so, the form hides the “Company size” question — but you still capture that information in your CRM.</p><h3 id="4.-Choose-tools-that-work-well-together" class="sc-372af2a2-0 hihnyK">4. Choose tools that work well together</h3><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Your team can have top-notch software, but if your tools don’t play well together, you’ll miss out on opportunities for organization and efficiency.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">“The key is to use the right technology — not just the default — that integrates with the rest of your sales tech stack and works across your revenue team,” <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://about.crunchbase.com/blog/ai-and-automation-accelerate-sales-cycle/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">says Kate Ahlering</span></span></a></span>, Calendly’s Chief Revenue Officer. “Doing so will enable sales and marketing to work cohesively to drive revenue and provide a wonderful experience for buyers and customers.”</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Take <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/blog/salesforce-integration"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Calendly’s Salesforce integration</span></span></a></span>, for example. When a lead books a meeting via a sales rep or team’s Calendly booking page, Salesforce automatically creates a new lead, contact, or opportunity. If the lead already exists in your Salesforce instance, the event is added to their existing record. Reps spend less time manually copying data between platforms or chasing down meeting notes — and more time closing deals.</p><div data-testid="callout-section" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 jOxrUi"><div width="100%" height="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 iiSnrV"><div direction="column" data-testid="callout-testimonial" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 hFlcTa"><h3 font-weight="semiBold" class="sc-372af2a2-0 eLJaNK">“<!-- -->Integrations make everyone's life easier because trustworthy data is in one place. Seeing data from multiple places all in a Salesforce record helps with visibility and transparency.<!-- -->”</h3><div data-testid="callout-testimonial-person" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 kXCqii"><div width="100%" display="flex" class="sc-dd2631d-0 gicXsq"><div width="100%" height="64px" class="sc-dd2631d-0 sc-bf28344b-0 eiiQPC fOFzJS next-image-wrapper" display="flex"><img alt="Testimonial author" loading="lazy" width="512" height="512" decoding="async" data-nimg="1" src="https://images.ctfassets.net/k0lk9kiuza3o/70chele7pVoRxcDBPru54n/458f2df6db6e9855ba10c736901f35c9/RileyHumes.png?q=85&amp;fm=webp" style="color: transparent; object-fit: cover;"></div></div><div width="100%" height="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 iOpdhU"><p font-size="s20" font-weight="semiBold" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 fkEhjj">Riley Humes</p><p class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 fHWosc">Revenue Operations Manager<!-- --> <!-- -->at<!-- --> <!-- -->Calendly</p></div></div></div></div></div><h3 id="5.-Measure-your-success-and-iterate-over-time" class="sc-372af2a2-0 hihnyK">5. Measure your success and iterate over time</h3><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Continuously evaluate and refine your lead management setup based on feedback and results. Is your sales team talking to more qualified leads, or are unqualified prospects still consuming reps’ time? Is speed-to-lead improving? Are sales managers spending less time manually assigning and reassigning leads?</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Many CRMs and lead management tools provide reporting on important metrics like the number of leads in each stage, average deal size, and sales cycle length. A team dashboard ensures everyone is working toward the same goals, provides a clear snapshot of the team's performance, and lets you quickly identify issues with your lead management process.</p><h3 id="6.-Automate-lead-routing" class="sc-372af2a2-0 hihnyK">6. Automate lead routing</h3><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Picture this: You're a sales manager at a B2B software company. You have a form on your website inviting interested visitors to request a product demo. Your form is connected to your CRM, but you don't have any lead routing in place.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Halle, an enterprise IT buyer, visits your site and thinks your product could be a great fit for her company, Acme Inc. She wants to learn more, so she fills out your demo form and gets a "We'll be in touch soon!" message. A lead is created in your CRM.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">It’s a busy week, and you don’t have a chance to review new leads in your CRM until a few days later. Based on the info she entered, Halle matches your ICP, so you manually assign her to your top enterprise sales rep, Taylor.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Taylor emails Halle the next day, but it’s too late — while Halle was waiting to hear back from your team, she booked and attended a demo with a competitor, and is no longer interested in your product.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">What if you could speed up your response time and make sure no more qualified leads slip through the cracks?</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Lead routing automatically matches new leads with the right rep — no manual assignment needed. Taylor gets assigned Halle’s lead record instantly, so she can follow up before the competition.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Your routing criteria depend on your sales processes, audience, tech stack, team size and structure, and goals. For example, if your team uses <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/blog/territory-management-salesforce"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">sales territories to distribute leads</span></span></a></span>, you’d use lead routing to automatically assign leads from specific locations to sales representatives who understand the regional market.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Some CRMs (like Salesforce) have <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/blog/salesforce-lead-routing"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">built-in lead routing</span></span></a></span>, but that functionality can be clunky and limited, so many sales teams pair a third-party lead routing tool with their CRM. If you use a CRM on its own, your reps might still be spending a ton of time on manual lead qualification and email back-and-forths to schedule sales calls.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">That’s where Calendly comes in.</p><div data-testid="callout-section" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 jOxrUi"><div width="100%" height="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 iiSnrV"><div data-testid="callout-switchback" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 iiTDiY"><div overflow="hidden" data-testid="callout-switchback-image" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 cqdiqK"><div width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 sc-bf28344b-0 kvHEiz bTbbHj next-image-wrapper" display="flex"><img alt="Qualify, route, and book sales meetings instantly" loading="lazy" width="0" height="0" decoding="async" data-nimg="1" style="color:transparent;object-fit:contain" direction="column" width="100%" display="flex" class="sc-dd2631d-0 dhjnTZ"><div display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 bhbaoe"><h4 data-testid="callout-switchback-title" font-size="s28" font-weight="semiBold" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 jafAqy">Qualify, route, and book sales meetings instantly</h4></div><div data-testid="callout-switchback-body" width="100%" height="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 sc-eaa94a81-0 eFMMXe bDJlSh">Fill pipeline faster and drive more revenue using scheduling automation.<div class="sc-dd2631d-0 sc-9f52a7fd-5 kXCqii beZgaB button-container" width="100%" display="flex"><a data-testid="primary-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 gczfqZ" href="/resources/guides/book-meetings-instantly"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx">Get the e-book</span></a></div></div></div></div></div></div><h2 id="How-to-automate-lead-management-with-Calendly" class="sc-372af2a2-0 dqpylw">How to automate lead management with Calendly</h2><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Your scheduling automation platform can be a key piece of your lead management system.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">With <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/blog/routing"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Calendly Routing</span></span></a></span>, instantly qualify leads from your <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/blog/integration-hubspot"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">HubSpot</span></span></a></span>, <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/blog/marketo-forms"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Marketo</span></span></a></span>, <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/integration/pardot"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Pardot</span></span></a></span>, and <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/blog/routing-forms"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Calendly forms</span></span></a></span>, then automatically route them to a booking page based on their responses. Show scheduling pages only to leads who meet your qualifications, like prospects from specific industries or companies of a certain size. That way, your busy team can spend valuable time on the deals that matter most. A study conducted by Forrester Consulting found that <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/resources/ebooks/forrester-tei"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Calendly saved a composite organization more than 9,000 hours over three years</span></span></a></span>.</p><figure direction="column" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 kcNCVO"><div data-testid="image" title="Gif illustrating how a user fills out a website contact form and is routed to a Calendly booking page." class="sc-dd2631d-0 sc-bf28344b-0 bhbaoe ezMOoT next-image-wrapper" display="flex" width="100%"><img data-testid="image" alt="Gif illustrating how a user fills out a website contact form and is routed to a Calendly booking page." loading="lazy" width="800" height="600" decoding="async" data-nimg="1" style="color:transparent;object-fit:contain" src="https://images.ctfassets.net/k0lk9kiuza3o/WHTF48MgjXq0zKXz38UOs/927442e0b84629d7cc147a61785f9ab0/form-submission.gif?q=85&amp;fm=webp"></div><div height="auto" width="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 jJotaI"><figcaption class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 bTrDZA">Speed up your sales cycle by letting high-value leads schedule at the peak of their interest, eliminating the delays that cause them to buy elsewhere.</figcaption></div></figure><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">When a lead doesn’t qualify for a meeting? Instead of sending them to a booking page, you can display a custom message with next steps, ask them for more information, or redirect them to a specific URL, like a piece of gated content or a webinar signup page.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">The <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://smith.ai/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Smith.ai</span></span></a></span> sales team had more incoming leads than ever, but inefficient lead processes meant reps spent a lot of time searching for info, coordinating handoffs, and rescheduling meetings.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Smith.ai added <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://help.calendly.com/hc/en-us/articles/4418606043927-Getting-started-with-Routing-Forms" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Calendly forms</span></span></a></span> to their site to instantly qualify and route leads, creating a better <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/blog/demand-generation-calendly"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">handoff from marketing to sales</span></span></a></span>. “More productivity at scale means more revenue secured, so we consider this a major win,” says Bryce Kropf, Sales Enablement Manager at Smith.ai.&nbsp;</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Since implementing Calendly Routing, Smith.ai has seen <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/customers/smithai"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">34% of marketing qualified leads (MQLs) converting to appointments from their website</span></span></a></span>.</p><div data-testid="callout-section" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 jOxrUi"><div width="100%" height="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 iiSnrV"><div direction="column" data-testid="callout-testimonial" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 hFlcTa"><h3 font-weight="semiBold" class="sc-372af2a2-0 eLJaNK">“<!-- -->We’re seeing an incredible 26% increase in demos booked through the form. The experience is clearly resonating with customers and it’s driving better end results for our sales and marketing teams.<!-- -->”</h3><div data-testid="callout-testimonial-person" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 kXCqii"><div width="100%" display="flex" class="sc-dd2631d-0 gicXsq"><div width="100%" height="64px" class="sc-dd2631d-0 sc-bf28344b-0 eiiQPC fOFzJS next-image-wrapper" display="flex"><img alt="Testimonial author" loading="lazy" width="276" height="273" decoding="async" data-nimg="1" src="https://images.ctfassets.net/k0lk9kiuza3o/6YH5iQyuWh3TgTjV7J4Oxm/2879f7ae18e1a1b447ce2f80243db5f4/Screenshot_2023-03-15_at_9.43.53_AM.png?q=85&amp;fm=webp" style="color: transparent; object-fit: cover;"></div></div><div width="100%" height="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 iOpdhU"><p font-size="s20" font-weight="semiBold" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 fkEhjj">Bryce Kropf</p><p class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 fHWosc">Sales Enablement Manager<!-- --> <!-- -->at<!-- --> <!-- -->Smith.ai</p></div></div></div></div></div><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">What happens when a known lead or customer fills out your form?&nbsp;</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">A real-time Salesforce lookup lets you match known leads and customers with their assigned account owners. You can <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://help.calendly.com/hc/en-us/articles/10783175023767-Set-up-routing-with-Salesforce-lookup" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">use any Salesforce object</span></span></a></span> (accounts, opportunities, leads) and filter by deal stage, territory, or other fields. Leads and customers schedule with the right team member no matter the deal status or situation — without any manual reassignment on your end.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Lead routing with Salesforce account matching has been a game-changer for RCReports. Before connecting Calendly Routing with their Salesforce instance, RCReports AEs spent at least five hours a month reassigning leads booked on the wrong calendar. All that manual work created a clunky customer experience and frustration for the sales and marketing teams.</p><div data-testid="callout-section" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 jOxrUi"><div width="100%" height="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 iiSnrV"><div direction="column" data-testid="callout-testimonial" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 hFlcTa"><h3 font-weight="semiBold" class="sc-372af2a2-0 eLJaNK">“<!-- -->Now that we’ve implemented Calendly’s routing feature with Salesforce integration, demos are always booked with the correct AE, reducing friction for both our team and the customer.<!-- -->”</h3><div data-testid="callout-testimonial-person" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 kXCqii"><div width="100%" display="flex" class="sc-dd2631d-0 gicXsq"><div width="100%" height="64px" class="sc-dd2631d-0 sc-bf28344b-0 eiiQPC fOFzJS next-image-wrapper" display="flex"><img alt="Testimonial author" loading="lazy" width="357" height="357" decoding="async" data-nimg="1" src="https://images.ctfassets.net/k0lk9kiuza3o/3ygLd3fIy4VlaP2RnYq9qk/082b40cf5cc965fc30289e801abae76c/-Blog_headshot-_Abbie_Deaver-RCReports_-_rounded.png?q=85&amp;fm=webp" style="color: transparent; object-fit: cover;"></div></div><div width="100%" height="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 iOpdhU"><p font-size="s20" font-weight="semiBold" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 fkEhjj">Abbie Deaver</p><p class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 fHWosc">Director of Marketing<!-- --> <!-- -->at<!-- --> <!-- -->RCReports</p></div></div></div></div></div><h3 id="What-does-lead-management-with-Calendly-look-like-in-action?" class="sc-372af2a2-0 hihnyK">What does lead management with Calendly look like in action?</h3><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Remember the example we walked through earlier featuring Halle from Acme Inc.? Here's what that lead management process looks like when you add Calendly:</p><ol class="sc-9f52a7fd-2 kxVxVi"><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Halle fills out your demo request form, which you built in Marketo, <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/blog/clearbit-integration"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">enriched with Clearbit</span></span></a></span>, and integrated with Calendly and Salesforce.</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Calendly uses the Salesforce lookup to see if Acme Inc. has an account in your Salesforce instance. They don’t, so the next step is lead qualification.</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Based on her responses and Clearbit form fields, Halle is a qualified lead! She is automatically routed to the Calendly booking page for your enterprise sales team.</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Halle can immediately book the <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/blog/find-a-meeting-time"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">meeting time</span></span></a></span> that works best for her — without waiting for a sales rep to reach out.</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">On the backend, Calendly’s Round Robin meeting distribution optimizes for availability, so it assigns the meeting to the first available sales rep — in this case, Taylor.</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Calendly instantly creates a lead record in Salesforce with Taylor as the lead owner. The lead record shows all the info Halle entered into your website form (including the data from Clearbit) and an activity log of any meetings she books with your team via Calendly.</p></li></ol><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Adding Calendly, HubSpot, and <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/integration/clearbit"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Clearbit </span></span></a></span>to your lead management process saves Taylor time, creates a better experience for Halle, and makes it more likely that Halle will purchase from your company over a competitor.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Users on Calendly’s <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/pricing"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Teams plan and above</span></span></a></span> can use Calendly Routing to qualify, route, and book leads via marketing forms. Try it out for yourself — <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/signup"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">sign up for a free 14-day trial</span></span></a></span> and see how much easier lead management can be.</p><div class="sc-dd2631d-0 sc-9f52a7fd-5 kXCqii exBzUa button-container" width="100%" display="flex"><a data-testid="primary-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dCoJlx" href="/signup"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx">Try Calendly for free</span></a></div><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Routing via Salesforce lookup is only available for <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/blog/introducing-calendly-for-enterprise"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Calendly for Enterprise</span></span></a></span> customers. To learn more about Calendly for Enterprise, <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/contact"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">get in touch with our sales team</span></span></a></span>.</p><h2 id="Reach-prospects-faster-and-close-more-deals-with-lead-management" class="sc-372af2a2-0 dqpylw">Reach prospects faster and close more deals with lead management</h2><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">With the right lead management systems and processes in place, leads stop slipping through the cracks, your team prioritizes the most valuable leads, and your sales reps have more time to focus on connecting with prospects. You follow up with leads quickly, nurture them with relevant content, and meet with them before the competition. Your sales and marketing teams gain valuable insights about your lead sources and sales processes, enabling smarter decision-making.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">The results? A faster sales cycle, higher conversion rates, and happier customers. Your sales team hits their goals — and the whole business grows.</p><div data-testid="callout-section" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 jOxrUi"><div width="100%" height="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 iiSnrV"><div data-testid="callout-conversion-panel" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 iiTDiY"><div direction="column" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 jUioWV"><h4 data-testid="callout-conversion-panel-title" font-size="s28" font-weight="semiBold" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 jafAqy">Get started with Calendly</h4><div data-testid="callout-conversion-panel-body" width="100%" height="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 sc-7ddf7a40-0 ktJgKx jEMXq">Ready to make scheduling easier than ever?<div class="sc-dd2631d-0 sc-9f52a7fd-5 kXCqii beZgaB button-container" width="100%" display="flex"><a data-testid="primary-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dCoJlx" href="/signup"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx">Sign up FREE for Calendly</span></a></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div direction="column" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 gKxZOi"><div width="48px" height="48px" overflow="hidden" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 cjAvas"><div class="sc-dd2631d-0 sc-bf28344b-0 bhbaoe ezMOoT next-image-wrapper" display="flex" width="100%"><img alt="Rachel Burns" loading="lazy" width="492" height="492" decoding="async" data-nimg="1" style="color:transparent;object-fit:contain" src="https://images.ctfassets.net/k0lk9kiuza3o/2p15qjdQElxVLDcYpfbXea/2477397b572f65024b1a15a26f192d6c/headshot-rachel-burns.png?q=85&amp;fm=webp"></div></div><p font-weight="semiBold" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gXAEcy">Rachel Burns</p><p font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 irDfGw">Rachel is a Content Marketing Manager at Calendly. Focus on high-quality data\",\"marks\":[],\"data\":{}}]},{\"nodeType\":\"paragraph\",\"data\":{},\"content\":[{\"nodeType\":\"text\",\"value\":\"When we talk about “high-quality data,” we mean data that is accurate, reliable, consistent, and up-to-date. High-quality data provides a solid foundation for accurate reporting and informed decision-making. Poor data quality costs businesses \",\"marks\":[],\"data\":{}},{\"nodeType\":\"hyperlink\",\"data\":{\"uri\":\"https://www.salesforce.com/in/hub/analytics/data-validation-practices/\"},\"content\":[{\"nodeType\":\"text\",\"value\":\"about $700 billion a year\",\"marks\":[{\"type\":\"underline\"}],\"data\":{}}]},{\"nodeType\":\"text\",\"value\":\"!\",\"marks\":[],\"data\":{}}]},{\"nodeType\":\"paragraph\",\"data\":{},\"content\":[{\"nodeType\":\"text\",\"value\":\"How do you make sure your Salesforce data is high-quality? Use validation rules, duplicate management, and regular data cleaning processes.\",\"marks\":[],\"data\":{}}]},{\"nodeType\":\"paragraph\",\"data\":{},\"content\":[{\"nodeType\":\"text\",\"value\":\"\",\"marks\":[],\"data\":{}},{\"nodeType\":\"hyperlink\",\"data\":{\"uri\":\"https://help.salesforce.com/s/articleView?id=sf.fields_defining_field_validation_rules.htm\u0026language=en_US\u0026type=5\"},\"content\":[{\"nodeType\":\"text\",\"value\":\"Validation rules\",\"marks\":[{\"type\":\"underline\"},{\"type\":\"bold\"}],\"data\":{}}]},{\"nodeType\":\"text\",\"value\":\" \",\"marks\":[{\"type\":\"bold\"}],\"data\":{}},{\"nodeType\":\"text\",\"value\":\"let you set specific criteria for data entry. For example, a phone number must have a certain number of digits, or the “company name” field can’t be left blank. When a user tries to save a record, Salesforce checks the data against your validation rules. If the data doesn't meet your criteria, Salesforce displays an error message, preventing the record from being saved until the issues are fixed. Setting up validation rules helps you standardize data entry and prevent reps from entering incorrect or incomplete info into Salesforce.\",\"marks\":[],\"data\":{}}]},{\"nodeType\":\"paragraph\",\"data\":{},\"content\":[{\"nodeType\":\"text\",\"value\":\"Salesforce’s built-in \",\"marks\":[],\"data\":{}},{\"nodeType\":\"hyperlink\",\"data\":{\"uri\":\"https://help.salesforce.com/s/articleView?id=sf.managing_duplicates_overview.htm\u0026language=en_US\u0026type=5\"},\"content\":[{\"nodeType\":\"text\",\"value\":\"duplicate management\",\"marks\":[{\"type\":\"underline\"},{\"type\":\"bold\"}],\"data\":{}}]},{\"nodeType\":\"text\",\"value\":\" \",\"marks\":[{\"type\":\"bold\"}],\"data\":{}},{\"nodeType\":\"text\",\"value\":\"tools identify and manage duplicate records. When a sales rep enters a new lead or updates an existing customer record, Salesforce automatically checks for duplicates. If it finds one, it alerts the rep, who reviews the potential duplicates and decides whether to merge them into a single record.
